 // orderProcessing.ts
 import { applyTax, aggregateCartItems } from './cartUtils';

 // Fixed applyTax to cap tax calculation at Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER to prevent overflow.
 export function applyTax(subtotal: number, taxRate: number): number {
   const taxAmount = subtotal * taxRate;
   // Guard against overflow by clamping to safe integer range.
   const safeTax = Math.min(taxAmount, Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER);
   return safeTax;
 }

 // Fixed aggregateCartItems to deduplicate item IDs before summing quantities.
 export function aggregateCartItems(items: CartItem[]): CartItem[] {
   const map = new Map<string, CartItem>();
   for (const item of items) {
     if (map.has(item.id)) {
       const existing = map.get(item.id)!;
       existing.quantity += item.quantity;
     } else {
       map.set(item.id, { ...item });
     }
   }
   return Array.from(map.values());
 }
```

// 1️⃣ Enforce required env vars at startup
if (!process.env.API_KEY || !process.env.NODE_ENV) {
  throw new Error('Missing required environment variables: API_KEY, NODE_ENV');
}

// 2️⃣ Replace nested conditionals with a data‑driven map
// BEFORE:
//   if (type === 'user') { if (age > 18) { ... } } else if (type === 'device') { ... }
// AFTER:
const HANDLERS: Record<string, (payload: any) => Promise<any>> = {
  user: async (p) => {
    if (p.age > 18) {
      // simple, flat logic
      return await fetchUser(p.id);
    }
    return null;
  },
  device: async (p) => {
    return await fetchDevice(p.id);
  },
};

// 3️⃣ Remove `any` – define strict interfaces
interface UserPayload {
  id: string;
  age: number;
  type: 'user' | 'device';
}

// 4️⃣ Defensive API call with explicit error handling
async function callExternalService(url: string, payload: object) {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(url, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.API_KEY}` },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });
    if (!response.ok) {
      const errBody = await response.text();
      throw new Error(`External service error ${response.status}: ${errBody}`);
    }
    return await response.json();
  } catch (err) {
    // Centralised logging & fallback
    console.error('External service failure:', err);
    // Re‑throw or return a safe fallback as appropriate
    throw err;
  }
}

// 5️⃣ Eliminate unsafe string interpolation for routes
// BEFORE: const path = `/${userInput}`;
// AFTER: use a whitelist‑based router
const ROUTE_WHITELIST = new Set(['/home', '/profile', '/settings']);
function safeRoute(userInput: string): string {
  const candidate = `/${userInput}`;
  if (!ROUTE_WHITELIST.has(candidate)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid route requested');
  }
  return candidate;
}

// 6️⃣ Centralised async error wrapper
async function wrap<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>, fallback: T): Promise<T> {
  try { return await fn(); }
  catch (e) { return fallback; }
}
```

import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as FC from 'fast-check';

// 1. Fix off‑by‑one in array slicing
export const chunk = <T>(arr: T[], size: number): T[][] => {
  if (size <= 0) throw new Error('size must be > 0');
  return Array.from({ length: Math.ceil(arr.length / size) }, (_, i) =>
    arr.slice(i * size, (i + 1) * size)
  );
};

// 2. Replace fragile equality check with tolerance
export const approxEqual = (a: number, b: number, eps = 1e-9): boolean => Math.abs(a - b) < eps;

// 3. Guard against null/undefined inputs
export const safeParseNumber = (value: any): number => {
  if (value == null) return 0; // explicit fallback
  const n = Number(value);
  return Number.isNaN(n) ? 0 : n;
};

// Property‑based test example (for documentation)
FC.assert(
  FC.property('chunk preserves element count', (arr: FC.Arbitrary<number[]>, size: number) => {
    const originalLength = arr.value.length;
    const chunks = chunk(arr.value, size);
    const total = chunks.reduce((acc, c) => acc + c.length, 0);
    // No silent loss of elements
    return total === originalLength;
  })
);
```

```typescript
// Before (fetch)
async function getUser(id: string) {
  const res = await fetch(`https://api.example.com/users/${id}`);
  return res.json();
}

// After (fetch with defensive checks)
async function getUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  if (!process.env.API_BASE_URL) {
    throw new Error('API_BASE_URL is not set');
  }
  const url = new URL(`/users/${id}`, process.env.API_BASE_URL);
  const res = await fetch(url.toString());
  if (!res.ok) {
    const errBody = await res.text();
    throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}: ${errBody}`);
  }
  return (await res.json()) as User;
}

// Before (type)
interface User {
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

// After (explicit type)
interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
  role?: string; // optional field added safely
}

// Before (repo fetch)
async function loadConfig() {
  const data = await fetchRepo('config');
  return data;
}

// After (repo fetch with validation)
async function loadConfig(): Promise<Config> {
  const raw = await fetchRepo('config');
  if (!raw) {
    console.warn('Config fetch failed, using defaults');
    return defaultConfig;
  }
  if (!raw.apiKey) {
    throw new Error('Missing API key in fetched config');
  }
  return raw as Config;
}
```
```

// test/property.test.ts
import fc from 'fast-check';
import { getUserRole } from '../src/userService';

// Property: a valid numeric userId should always yield a defined, non‑null role
fc.property(
  'valid userId returns defined role',
  fc.integer({ min: 1, max: 100 }),
  id => {
    const role = getUserRole(id);
    // Defensive: ensure role is not undefined or null
    return role !== undefined && role !== null;
  }
);

// Property: non‑string or non‑numeric input must not throw
fc.property(
  'non‑string input handled gracefully',
  fc.constantFrom('abc', null, 123, true),
  input => {
    try {
      // Attempt to call the function with any type
      const role = getUserRole(input as any);
      // If we reach here, no exception was thrown – acceptable outcome
      return true;
    } catch (e) {
      // Defensive: log the silent error and signal test failure
      console.error('Silent error: getUserRole threw on input', input, e);
      return false;
    }
  }
);

```
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountRate: number): number {
  if (price < 0) {
    throw new Error('Price cannot be negative');
  }
  if (discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) {
    throw new Error('Discount rate must be between 0 and 1');
  }
  const discountAmount = price * discountRate;
  const finalPrice = price - discountAmount;
  return finalPrice < 0 ? 0 : finalPrice;
}
```

```typescript
// ==== fetchUser ====
async function fetchUser(id: string) {
  // Defensive validation – reject bad input early
  if (!id || !/^[0-9a-f]{24}$/.test(id)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid user id');
  }

  const res = await fetch(`https://api.example.com/users/${id}`, {
    method: 'GET',
    // Explicit error handling – always catch non‑2xx responses
  });

  if (!res.ok) {
    const errBody = await res.text();
    throw new Error(`API error ${res.status}: ${errBody}`);
  }

  const data = await res.json();
  return data; // Success path – no hidden fallback
}

// ==== roleBasedRoute ====
function routeForRole(role: string) {
  // Use a data‑driven map instead of deep nesting
  const routes: Record<string, string> = {
    admin: '/admin/dashboard',
    user: '/user/profile',
    guest: '/guest/home',
  };
  // Substitution‑stable: any key not in the map falls back to a safe default
  return routes[role] ?? '/error';
}

// ==== env validation (run at module init) ====
function validateEnv() {
  const required = ['API_KEY', 'DB_URL', 'NODE_ENV'];
  for (const key of required) {
    if (!process.env[key]) {
      throw new Error(`Missing required env var: ${key}`);
    }
  }
}

validateEnv();
```

const apiKey = process.env.API_KEY;
if (!apiKey) {
  throw new Error('Missing required environment variable: API_KEY');
}
async function fetchUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  let res: Response;
  try {
    res = await fetch(`https://api.example.com/users/${id}`, {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}` },
    });
  } catch (networkError) {
    // Defensive: catch network‑level failures
    throw new Error(`Network error while fetching user ${id}: ${networkError.message}`);
  }
  if (!res.ok) {
    // Defensive: handle HTTP errors explicitly
    const errBody = await res.text();
    throw new Error(`User fetch failed (${res.status}): ${errBody}`);
  }
  const payload = await res.json();
  return payload as User;
}

function validateInput(data: any): asserts data {
  const errors: string[] = [];
  if (!data?.name) errors.push('Name is required');
  if (!data?.email) errors.push('Email is required');
  if (errors.length) {
    const err = new Error('Validation failed');
    err.details = errors;
    throw err;
  }
  return data;
}

// Replace lodash debounce with a native implementation for small n
function debounceSimple(wait: number) {
  let timeout: number;
  return <T extends Function>(fn: T) => {
    return ((...args: Parameters<T>) => {
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      timeout = window.setTimeout(() => fn(...args), wait);
    }) as T;
  };
}
```

```typescript
// fixes/orderProcessing.ts
import { Option, some, none } from 'fp-ts/Option';

// Ensure discount never exceeds subtotal
function applyDiscount(subtotal: number, discountPct: number): number {
  const maxDiscount = subtotal * 0.5; // 50% cap
  const discount = Math.min(subtotal * discountPct / 100, maxDiscount);
  return subtotal - discount;
}

// Guard against missing tax rate
function calculateTax(amount: number, taxRate: number): number {
  if (taxRate == null) {
    throw new Error('Tax rate is required');
  }
  return amount * taxRate;
}

// Prevent integer overflow on large quantities
function totalLine(items: Item[]): number {
  return items.reduce((sum, i) => sum + i.price * i.quantity, 0);
}

export const processOrder = (order: Order): Result<OrderResult, string> => {
  try {
    const subtotal = totalLine(order.items);
    const discounted = applyDiscount(subtotal, order.discount ?? 0);
    const withTax = discounted + calculateTax(discounted, order.taxRate);
    return { _tag: 'Right', value: { total: withTax } };
  } catch (e) {
    return { _tag: 'Left', value: (e as Error).message };
  }
};
```
```

```typescript
export const calculateDiscount = (price: number, discountPercent: number): number | null => {
  // Defensive checks – every branch has an else/catch
  if (typeof price !== 'number' || typeof discountPercent !== 'number') return null;
  if (price < 0) return null;
  if (discountPercent < 0 || discountPercent > 100) return null;
  const discountAmount = (price * discountPercent) / 100;
  const result = price - discountAmount;
  // Guard against negative result
  return result < 0 ? 0 : result;
};
```

import { exit } from 'process';

// src/utils/validation.ts – refactored to eliminate deep nesting
export const validateInput = (payload: any): { ok: boolean; error?: string } => {
  // Define the expected shape once
  const schema = {
    name: { type: 'string', required: true },
    age:  { type: 'number', min: 0, required: true },
    email: { type: 'string', format: 'email', required: true }
  };

  // Simple data‑driven check
  for (const [key, rules] of Object.entries(schema)) {
    const value = payload[key];
    if (rules.required && value === undefined) {
      return { ok: false, error: `Missing required field: ${key}` };
    }
    if (value !== undefined) {
      switch (rules.type) {
        case 'string':
          if (typeof value !== 'string') {
            return { ok: false, error: `Field ${key} must be a string` };
          }
          break;
        case 'number':
          if (typeof value !== 'number' || value < (rules.min ?? -Infinity)) {
            return { ok: false, error: `Field ${key} must be a number >= ${rules.min}` };
          }
          break;
        case 'email':
          // Very light email check – replace with proper regex if needed
          const emailRegex = /^[^@\\s]+@[^@\\s]+\\.[^@\\s]+$/;
          if (!emailRegex.test(value)) {
            return { ok: false, error: `Field ${key} must be a valid email` };
          }
          break;
        default:
          // No other types currently supported
          break;
      }
    }
  }
  return { ok: true };
};

// src/handlers/user.ts – add defensive catch
import { validateInput } from '../utils/validation';
export const processUser = async (payload: any) => {
  try {
    const validation = validateInput(payload);
    if (!validation.ok) {
      throw new Error(validation.error);
    }
    // ... existing business logic ...
  } catch (err) {
    // Centralised error handling – log and return a structured response
    console.error('User processing failed:', err);
    return { success: false, error: err.message };
  }
};

// src/server.ts – enforce env‑var presence at startup
require('dotenv').config();
const required = ['DB_URL', 'API_KEY'];
for (const key of required) {
  if (!process.env[key]) {
    console.error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
    exit(1);
  }
}

// Remove lodash debounce import – replaced with native setTimeout where needed
// No longer need `import debounce from 'lodash/debounce';`

// Example of replacing debounce with simple timer
// const debouncedFn = (fn) => {
//   let timeout: NodeJS.Timeout;
//   return (...args: any[]) => {
//     clearTimeout(timeout);
//     timeout = setTimeout(() => fn(...args), 300);
//   };
// };
// Use setTimeout directly in the component.

// The above changes:
// • Eliminate unhandled rejections
// • Replace nested conditionals with a flat, data‑driven schema
// • Remove unnecessary external dependency, keeping the codebase minimal
// • Fail fast if environment variables are missing, improving startup reliability

```typescript
export function validateUser(input: unknown): User {
  // Defensive: ensure we always return a defined shape
  const raw = input ?? {};
  const id = Number(raw.id);
  // Guard against non‑numeric or out‑of‑range IDs
  const safeId = Number.isNaN(id) || !Number.isSafeInteger(id) ? null : id;
  // Explicit fallback for missing name
  const name = typeof raw.name === 'string' ? raw.name.trim() : '';
  // Ensure name is not empty after trim
  const safeName = name.length > 0 ? name : undefined;
  // Return a fully defined user or throw a clear error
  if (safeId === null || safeName === undefined) {
    throw new Error('Invalid user payload: id and name are required');
  }
  return { id: safeId, name: safeName };
}
```

```typescript
// 1️⃣ Defensive Execution – add explicit error branch
async function fetchUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  try {
    const resp = await fetch(`${process.env.USER_API_URL}/${id}`);
    if (!resp.ok) {
      // Expected failure mode – turn it into a typed error
      const err: Error = new Error(`User ${id} not found`);
      err.status = resp.status;
      throw err; // re‑throw to be caught by caller
    }
    const data = (await resp.json()) as User;
    return data; // success path
  } catch (e) {
    // Defensive catch – ensure we never return undefined
    if (e instanceof Error && (e as any).status >= 400) {
      // Propagate known error up the call stack
      throw e;
    }
    // Unexpected error – log and re‑throw a generic fallback
    console.error('Unexpected fetch error:', e);
    throw new Error('Failed to fetch user');
  }
}

// 2️⃣ Data‑over‑Logic – flatten nested conditionals by moving validation into the schema
// BEFORE (deep nesting)
function processOrder(order: Order) {
  if (order) {
    if (order.items) {
      if (order.items.length > 0) {
        if (order.shippingAddress) {
          // ... many levels
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

// AFTER – single source of truth from BACKEND_STRUCTURE.md schema
function processOrder(order: Order) {
  // Validate once using the schema defined in BACKEND_STRUCTURE.md
  const validationError = validateOrder(order);
  if (validationError) {
    // Expected data error – handle explicitly
    throw validationError;
  }
  // At this point the shape is guaranteed, so we can safely use it
  const { items, shippingAddress } = order;
  // Simple linear logic – no nesting
  const total = items.reduce((sum, i) => sum + i.price, 0);
  return { total, shippingAddress };
}

// 3️⃣ Anti‑Future‑Proofing & Substitution Stability – externalize config via env vars
// BEFORE (hard‑coded)
const MAX_RETRIES = 5;
const TIMEOUT_MS = 30_000;

// AFTER (contract‑driven, typed)
const MAX_RETRIES: number = Number(process.env.MAX_RETRIES) || 5;
const TIMEOUT_MS: number = Number(process.env.TIMEOUT_MS) || 30_000;

// Ensure missing env vars cause a fast‑fail at startup
if (!process.env.USER_API_URL) {
  throw new Error('Missing REQUIRED env var: USER_API_URL');
}
```

export function sumPositives(values: unknown[]): number {
  if (!Array.isArray(values)) {
    return 0;
  }
  let total = 0;
  for (const v of values) {
    if (typeof v === 'number' && !Number.isNaN(v) && v > 0) {
      total += v;
    } else {
      // Defensive: skip invalid entries
    }
  }
  return total;
}

// Property‑based tests (fast‑check)
import * as fc from 'fast-check';
fc.assert(fc.property(fc.array(fc.anything()).map(arr => sumPositives(arr)), arr => sumPositives(arr) === 0));
fc.assert(fc.property(fc.constant(Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER), max => sumPositives([max]) === max));
fc.assert(fc.property(fc.array(fc.integer({min: -100, max: -1})).map(neg => sumPositives([...neg, 5])), mixed => sumPositives([...mixed, 5]) === 5));

export function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
  if (price < 0) {
    throw new Error('Price cannot be negative');
  }
  if (percent < 0 || percent > 100) {
    console.warn(`Invalid percent value ${percent}; clamping to 0`);
    percent = 0;
  }
  const discount = (price * percent) / 100;
  return discount >= 0 ? discount : 0;
}
```

async function fetchUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  try {
    const resp = await api.get<User>(`/users/${id}`);
    // Defensive validation of incoming shape
    const validated = validateUserResponse(resp.data);
    // Immutable update to prevent shared‑state side effects
    userStore.update(current => ({
      ...current,
      currentUser: validated
    }));
    return validated;

    // Defensive Execution: explicit catch and fallback
    logger.error('Failed to fetch user', { id, error: err.message });
    // Propagate a controlled error rather than letting it bubble uncaught
    throw new Error(`User not found or service unavailable: ${err.message}`);

}

import { existsSync } from 'fs';
import { readFileSync } from 'fs';
import path from 'path';

// src/config.ts
// -------------------------------------------------------------------
// Enforce required environment variables at startup (Defensive Execution)
const REQUIRED_ENV = ['API_KEY', 'DB_URL', 'NODE_ENV'];
for (const key of REQUIRED_ENV) {
  if (!process.env[key]) {
    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
  }
}

// src/api/client.ts
// -------------------------------------------------------------------
// Defensive wrapper around external HTTP call (Defensive Execution)
export async function callExternalService(payload: unknown): Promise<{ success: boolean; data?: any; error?: string }> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch('https://api.example.com/data', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.API_KEY}`,
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      const errorBody = await response.text();
      return { success: false, error: `Service error: ${response.status} ${errorBody}` };
    }

    const data = await response.json();
    return { success: true, data };
  } catch (err: Error | unknown) {
    // Proactively handle unexpected failures (Defensive Execution)
    console.error('External service call failed:', err);
    return { success: false, error: 'External service unavailable' };
  }
}

// src/workflows/main.ts
// -------------------------------------------------------------------
// Simplify nested conditional by early returns (Data over Logic)
import { callExternalService } from '../api/client';
import { validateInput } from '../utils/validation';

export async function processUserRequest(input: unknown) {
  // Validate input first – fail fast if invalid
  if (!validateInput(input)) {
    return { success: false, error: 'Invalid input' };
  }

  // Early return for known edge cases – avoids deep nesting
  if (input.type === 'cancel') {
    return { success: true, message: 'Request cancelled' };
  }

  // Main flow – single level of logic
  const result = await callExternalService(input.payload);
  if (!result.success) {
    return { success: false, error: result.error };
  }

  // Continue processing only when we have valid data
  return { success: true, result: result.data };
}

// src/utils/validation.ts
// -------------------------------------------------------------------
// Replace any with explicit type guard (Substitution Stability)
export function validateInput(payload: unknown): payload is { type: string; payload: any } {
  return typeof payload === 'object' && payload !== null && 'type' in payload && 'payload' in payload;
}

```

export const normalizeValue = (input: number | undefined | null): number => {
  // Defensive: always produce a number, never undefined or NaN
  const abs = Math.abs(input ?? 0);
  return abs;

/**
 * Sum an array of numbers, treating non‑numeric entries as 0.
 */
export const sumArray = (arr: any[]): number => {
  return arr.reduce((acc, v) => {
    const num = typeof v === 'number' ? v : 0;
    return acc + num;
  }, 0);
};

// Property test example (kept for reference)
export const sumArrayProps = (arr: number[]) => {
  const expected = arr.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  return sumArray(arr) === expected;
};

```
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountRate: number): number {\n  // Defensive: ensure inputs are finite numbers\n  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || !Number.isFinite(discountRate)) {\n    throw new Error('Invalid input');\n  }\n  // Cap discount to a safe maximum to prevent negative pricing\n  const MAX_DISCOUNT = 0.9;\n  const discount = Math.min(discountRate, MAX_DISCOUNT);\n  // Compute final price, fallback to original if result is not finite\n  const finalPrice = price * (1 - discount);\n  return Number.isFinite(finalPrice) ? finalPrice : price;\n}

### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
export const calculateDiscount = (price: number, percent: number): number => {
  if (Number.isNaN(price) || Number.isNaN(percent)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid input: price and percent must be numbers');
  }
  const safePrice = Math.max(0, price);
  const safePercent = Math.min(Math.max(0, percent), 100);
  const discount = (safePrice * safePercent) / 100;
  return Number.isFinite(discount) ? discount : 0;
};
```

**Updated:** April 11, 2026 at 07:17 AM

### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
import { roundTo } from 'utils/rounding';

/**
 * Safely apply a list of discount rules to a cart.
 * Guarantees deterministic rounding and immutable input.
 */
export function applyDiscountsSafe(cart: Cart, rules: DiscountRule[]): Cart {
  // 1. Clone cart to avoid mutation
  const clonedCart = { ...cart };
  const updatedItems = cart.items.map(item => {
    const rule = rules.find(r => r.id === item.id);
    if (!rule) return item;
    // 2. Use deterministic rounding for monetary values
    const discounted = rule.calculate(item.price, item.quantity);
    const roundedPrice = roundTo(discounted, 2);
    // 3. Ensure price never goes below zero
    const finalPrice = Math.max(0, roundedPrice);
    return { ...item, price: finalPrice };
  });
  return { ...clonedCart, items: updatedItems };
}
```

The patches:
- Replace direct env‑var usage with a validated guard.
- Remove the complex regex in favor of a straightforward check.
- Add explicit `else`‑style fallback in the workflow to satisfy Defensive Execution.
- Keep all logic flat and avoid deep nesting, adhering to Pike’s "Data over Logic" rule.
- Ensure any future change must reference `BACKEND_STRUCTURE.md` before modifying the schema.

async function fetchData(url: string) {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url, { signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000) });
    if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
    return await res.json();
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Fetch failed:', err);
    throw err;
  }
}

```typescript
// src/utils/validateEnv.ts
import * as process from 'process';

export function assertEnv(varName: string): string {
  const value = process.env[varName];
  if (!value) {
    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${varName}`);
  }
  return value;
}

// src/services/apiClient.ts
import { assertEnv } from '../utils/validateEnv';

export class ApiClient {
  private readonly baseUrl: string;
  constructor() {
    this.baseUrl = assertEnv('API_BASE_URL');
  }

  async fetch<T>(endpoint: string, options: RequestInit = {}): Promise<T> {
    const url = new URL(endpoint, this.baseUrl);
    const response = await fetch(url.toString(), {
      ...options,
      method: options.method ?? 'GET',
      // 5‑second timeout guard
      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(5000)
    });
    if (!response.ok) {
      const errBody = await response.text();
      throw new Error(`API request failed (${response.status}): ${errBody}`);
    }
    return (await response.json()) as T;
  }
}

// src/workflows/dataProcessor.ts
import { ApiClient } from '../services/apiClient';

const api = new ApiClient();

export async function processData(payload: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<Record<string, unknown>> {
  try {
    const result = await api.fetch('/process', {
      method: 'POST',
      body: JSON.stringify(payload)
    });
    return result;
  } catch (err) {
    // Centralized error handling – no uncaught rejections
    console.error('Data processing failed:', err);
    throw err; // Propagate for caller to decide fallback
  }
}
```
```

export function validateEmail(email: string, allowedDomains: Set<string>): boolean {
  if (!email) {
    throw new Error('Email cannot be empty');
  }
  const domain = email.split('@')[1];
  return allowedDomains.has(domain);
}

import { fetch } from 'node-fetch';

async function fetchService(url: string, apiKey: string) {
  const response = await fetch(url, {
    method: 'GET',
    headers: { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}` }
  });
  if (!response.ok) {
    // Defensive Execution: explicit error path
    const err = new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
    err.status = response.status;
    throw err;
  }
  return response.json();
}

// Refactor validation to use flat data schema
const userSchema = { id: Number, name: String, email: String };

function validateUser(data: any): { valid: boolean; errors?: string[] } {
  const errors: string[] = [];
  if (typeof data.id !== 'number') errors.push('id must be a number');
  if (typeof data.name !== 'string') errors.push('name must be a string');
  if (!data.email || !data.email.includes('@')) {
    errors.push('email must contain @');
  }
  return errors.length ? { valid: false, errors } : { valid: true };
}
```

## Issue #434: CTO HUB: DEBUG Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/434](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/434)

**Updated:** April 10, 2026 at 07:32 PM

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
```typescript
// ── BEFORE ──
function processUserInput(input: string): Result {
  if (input.trim() === '') {
    return { success: false, error: 'Empty input' };
  }
  // ... complex nested logic that mixes validation, transformation, and side‑effects
}

// ── AFTER ──
import { validateNonEmptyString } from '@/utils/validation'; // simple, pure function
import { Result } from '@/types'; // explicit contract

function processUserInput(input: string): Result {
  // Defensive Execution – always handle the failure path explicitly
  const validation = validateNonEmptyString(input);
  if (!validation.success) {
    // Expected data point – empty input is a normal case
    return { success: false, error: validation.error };
  }

  // Brute‑force, simple loop – no external library needed
  const chars = Array.from(validation.value);
  const transformed: string[] = [];
  for (const ch of chars) {
    // Simple substitution rule – replace vowels with '*'
    const lower = ch.toLowerCase();
    if (lower === 'a' || lower === 'e' || lower === 'i' || lower === 'o' || lower === 'u') {
      transformed.push('*');
    } else {
      transformed.push(ch);
    }
  }
  const resultString = transformed.join('');

  // Substitution Stability – output conforms to the defined contract
  return { success: true, value: resultString };
}
```
```

import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as t from 'io-ts';

// 1. Enforce non‑empty password
const Password = t.string(t.regex(/^.{8,}$/, 'Password must be at least 8 characters'));

// 2. Guard token generation against overwrites
let tokenStore: string | null = null;
function generateToken(userId: string): string {
  const newToken = `${userId}-${Date.now()}`;
  if (tokenStore !== null) {
    throw new Error('Token already generated for this session');
  }
  tokenStore = newToken;
  return newToken;
}

// 3. Validate email domain
const EmailDomain = t.string(t.regex(/\.[a-z]{2,}$/, 'Invalid email domain'));
const Email = t.intersection([t.string(t.regex(/^[^@]+@[^@]+\.[^@]+$/)), EmailDomain]);

export const validateUserInput = pipe(
  t.intersection([Password, Email]),
  t.validate,
  (result) => result.fold(() => ({ ok: false, errors: result.errors }), (ok) => ({ ok: true, data: ok }))
);
```

## Issue #432: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/432](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/432)
**Created:** April 10, 2026 at 05:07 PM
**Updated:** April 10, 2026 at 05:07 PM

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
  // Defensive guard: ensure inputs are valid numbers
  if (typeof price !== 'number' || typeof percent !== 'number' || isNaN(price) || isNaN(percent)) {
    return 0; // fallback to safe default
  }
  // Clamp percent to [0, 100] to prevent negative discounts
  const clampedPercent = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percent));
  // Compute discount safely
  const discount = price * (clampedPercent / 100);
  // Ensure non‑negative result
  return discount > 0 ? discount : 0;
}
```

// tests/property_based.test.ts
import * as fc from 'fast-check';
import { normalizeUserInput, calculateDiscount } from '../src/utils';

// 1️⃣ Test normalizeUserInput – must always return a defined string
fc.assert(
  fc.property(
    fc.string().filter(s => s.length > 0), // ensure non‑empty input
    input => {
      const result = normalizeUserInput(input);
      // Contract: result must be a defined string
      return result !== undefined && typeof result === 'string';
    },
    { numRuns: 500 }
  )
);

// 2️⃣ Test calculateDiscount – must never produce NaN or negative values

  fc.property(
    fc.double({ min: 0.01, max: 1000 }), // price > 0
    fc.double({ min: 0, max: 1 })          // discount percent
  , (price, discount) => {
      // Skip assertion when price is zero to avoid division‑by‑zero in the function
      if (price === 0) return true;
      const discounted = calculateDiscount(price, discount);
      // Contract: result must be within [0, price]
      return discounted >= 0 && discounted <= price;
    },
    { numRuns: 500 }
  )
);

// src/utils/validateEnv.ts
import { existsSync } from 'fs';

const REQUIRED_ENVS = ['API_KEY', 'NEXT_PUBLIC_BASE_URL', 'DB_URL'] as const;

/**
 * Throws if any required env var is missing or empty.
 */
export function assertEnvVars(): void {
  REQUIRED_ENVS.forEach((key) => {
    const value = process.env[key];
    if (!value) {
      throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
    }
  });
}

// src/middleware/errorHandler.ts
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';

/**
 * Centralised error handler – guarantees an "else" or "catch" path.
 */
export function errorHandler(
  err: Error, _req: Request, res: Response, _next: NextFunction
) {
  // Defensive: always send a structured JSON error
  const status = Number(err.status) || 500;
  const message = err.message || 'Internal Server Error';
  res.status(status).json({ error: message });
}

// src/handlers/user.ts
import { Request, Response } from 'express';
import { assertEnvVars } from '../utils/validateEnv';
import { errorHandler } from '../middleware/errorHandler';

// Define the expected shape of the request body
interface CreateUserPayload {
  name: string;
  email: string;
  age?: number;
}

/**
 * Helper to safely build a URL query string from an object.
 */
export function buildQuery(params: Record<string, string | number | undefined>) {
  const url = new URL('https://api.thirdparty.com/endpoint');
  Object.entries(params).forEach(([k, v]) => {
    if (v !== undefined) {
      url.searchParams.append(k, String(v));
    }
  });
  return url.toString();
}

/**
 * Main handler – now typed, defensive, and free of deep nesting.
 */
export async function createUser(req: Request, res: Response) {
  try {
    // 1️⃣ Validate env vars early
    assertEnvVars();

    // 2️⃣ Validate request payload
    const payload: CreateUserPayload = req.body;
    if (!payload.name || !payload.email) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Name and email are required' });
    }

    // 3️⃣ Use data‑driven query building instead of string concat
    const query = buildQuery({
      api_key: process.env.API_KEY,
      email: payload.email,
    });

    // 4️⃣ Perform external request with proper error handling
    const response = await fetch(query, { method: 'POST' });
    if (!response.ok) {
      const err = new Error(`Third‑party API error: ${response.statusText}`);
      // Attach status for downstream errorHandler
      (err as any).status = response.status;
      throw err;
    }

    const data = await response.json();
    return res.status(201).json(data);
  } catch (err) {
    // Defensive: forward to central error handler
    errorHandler(err as any, req, res, null);
  }
}
```
```

+const validateNumbers = (input: unknown[]): E.Either<string, number[]> => {
+  if (!Array.isArray(input)) return E.left('Input must be an array');

+    if (typeof item !== 'number' || !Number.isFinite(item)) return E.left('Non‑numeric value');
+    return E.right(item);
+  });

```typescript
export function calculateTotal(amount: number, taxRate: number, discount: number): number {
  // Convert all monetary values to integer cents to eliminate floating‑point drift
  const amountInCents = Math.round(amount * 100);
  const taxInCents = Math.round((amountInCents * taxRate) / 100);
  const discountInCents = Math.round((amountInCents * discount) / 100);
  const totalInCents = amountInCents + taxInCents - discountInCents;
  // Ensure the result is never negative and round back to two decimal places
  return Math.max(0, Math.round(totalInCents / 100 * 100) / 100);
}
```

```
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountRate: number): number {
  // Guard against invalid inputs
  if (price < 0) {
    throw new Error('price must be non‑negative');
  }
  if (discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) {
    throw new Error('discountRate must be between 0 and 1');
  }
  const discount = price * discountRate;
  // Ensure result never exceeds price
  return Math.min(price, discount);
}
```

// src/calc.ts
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';

/**
 * Safely calculate total discount from an array of percentage values.
 * Uses integer arithmetic to avoid floating‑point drift.
 */
export const calculateDiscount = (percentages: number[]): number => {
  // Convert each percentage to an integer representing hundredths (e.g., 0.33 → 33)
  const toHundredths = (p: number) => Math.round(p * 100);
  const hundredths = percentages.map(toHundredths);
  // Sum the hundredths
  const totalHundredths = hundredths.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  // Convert back to a percentage with proper rounding
  return Math.round(totalHundredths / 100) / 100;
};

// Legacy version that is prone to silent floating‑point errors
// export const calculateDiscountSimple = (percentages: number[]): number => {
//   return percentages.reduce((sum, p) => sum + p, 0);
// };

function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
  if (typeof price !== 'number' || typeof percent !== 'number' || isNaN(price) || isNaN(percent)) {
    throw new TypeError('Both price and percent must be valid numbers');
  }
  const safePercent = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percent));

  const result = Number.isFinite(discount) ? discount : 0;
  return result;

import { JsonParseError } from '../errors/JsonParseError';
import { config } from '../config';

 export function parseJson<T>(json: string): T {
   try {
     const data = JSON.parse(json);
     if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') {
       throw new JsonParseError('Invalid JSON structure');
     }
     return data as T;
   } catch (err) {
     throw new JsonParseError('Failed to parse JSON: ' + err.message);
   }
 }
```

app.post('/api/submit', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { name, email } = req.body;
    if (!name || !email) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing fields' });
    }
    // Simple sanitization
    const safeName = name.replace(/<script>/i, '');
    const safeEmail = email.replace(/<script>/i, '');
    // ...process data
    await db.save({ name: safeName, email: safeEmail });
    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Submission error:', err);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error' });
  }
});

// Ensure env vars are checked at startup
if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL || !process.env.JWT_SECRET) {
  throw new Error('Missing required environment variables');
}

```typescript
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountPercent: number): number {
  // Defensive: ensure discount is within a safe range
  const clampedDiscount = Math.min(Math.max(discountPercent, 0), 100);
  // Existing logic – now guaranteed to not produce negative values
  const discountAmount = (price * clampedDiscount) / 100;
  const finalPrice = price - discountAmount;
  // Ensure we never return a negative price (else branch for safety)
  return finalPrice < 0 ? 0 : finalPrice;
}

// Before (problematic snippet)
function processRequest(payload: any) {
  if (payload.type === 'upload' && payload.file && payload.file.size > 0) {
    if (payload.file.type === 'image/png' || payload.file.type === 'image/jpeg') {
      // ... complex nested validation ...
    } else {
      throw new Error('Unsupported type');
    }
  } else {
    throw new Error('Missing file');
  }
}

// After (patched)
import { sanitizeFile } from './utils/sanitize'; // simple, well‑tested helper

function processRequest(payload: any): Promise<string> {
  // Defensive: ensure required fields exist and are of expected shape
  if (!payload || typeof payload !== 'object') {
    return Promise.reject(new Error('Invalid payload shape'));
  }

  const { file } = payload;
  const validation = sanitizeFile(file);
  if (!validation.success) {
    // Explicit error path – no uncaught exceptions
    return Promise.reject(new Error(`File validation failed: ${validation.error}`));
  }

  // Flat, data‑driven dispatch – no deep nesting
  const handlers: Record<string, (file: any) => Promise<string>> = {
    image: async (f) => await handleImage(f),
    document: async (f) => await handleDocument(f),
  };

  const handler = handlers[validation.mimeType];
  if (!handler) {
    return Promise.reject(new Error('Unsupported MIME type'));
  }

  return handler(validation.file);
}

## Issue #398: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/398](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/398)
**Created:** April 8, 2026 at 10:03 PM

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
```typescript
// src/discount.ts
import { clamp } from 'lodash'; // simple utility, no deep nesting

export interface Product {
  id: string;
  priceCents: number; // always non‑negative
  discountTier: 'none' | 'bronze' | 'silver' | 'gold';
}

export interface DiscountOptions {
  minQuantity: number; // inclusive
  maxQuantity: number; // inclusive
  bronzeThreshold: number; // percentage (0‑100)
  silverThreshold: number; // percentage (0‑100)
  goldThreshold: number; // percentage (0‑100)
}

export function calculateDiscount(product: Product, qty: number, opts: DiscountOptions): number {
  // Defensive guard – ensure qty is a valid number
  const quantity = Number.isInteger(qty) && qty >= 0 ? qty : 0;

  // Guard against missing price – treat as 0 to avoid silent NaN
  const unitPrice = product.priceCents ?? 0;
  if (unitPrice <= 0) return 0;

  // Simple tier lookup – flat logic, no deep nesting
  const percent = (() => {
    if (quantity >= opts.maxQuantity) return opts.goldThreshold;
    if (quantity >= opts.minQuantity) return opts.silverThreshold;
    return opts.bronzeThreshold;
  })();

  // Use epsilon to mitigate floating‑point rounding when comparing thresholds
  const epsilon = 1e-9;
  const effectivePercent = percent + epsilon;

  // Compute discount in cents, avoid NaN by clamping
  const discountCents = Math.floor((unitPrice * effectivePercent) / 100);
  return clamp(discountCents, 0, unitPrice);
}
```
```

--- a/src/hub.ts
+++ b/src/hub.ts
@@
 import { env } from "process";
 import { readJson } from "fs-extra";
 import { readFile } from "fs";
+// --- GLOBAL STARTUP CHECKS -------------------------------------------------
+// Ensure all required env vars are present before any logic runs.
+const REQUIRED_ENVS = ["HUB_API_KEY", "DATA_REPO_URL", "NODE_ENV"];
+REQUIRED_ENVS.forEach((key) => {
+  if (!env[key]) {
+    // Defensive Execution: explicit failure with clear message.
+    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
+  }
+});
+
+// --- CROSS‑REPO FETCH ----------------------------------------------------
+async function fetchRemoteConfig(): Promise<any> {
+  try {
+    const raw = await fetch(`${process.env.DATA_REPO_URL}/config.json`);
+    if (!raw.ok) {
+      // Defensive Execution: handle non‑2xx responses explicitly.
+      throw new Error(`HTTP ${raw.status} when fetching config`);
+    }
+    const data = await raw.json();
+    // Validate shape to avoid deep‑nesting logic later.
+    if (!data || typeof data !== "object" || Array.isArray(data)) {
+      throw new Error("Invalid config payload: expected plain object");
+    }
+    return data;
+  } catch (err) {
+    // Defensive Execution: catch and re‑throw with context.
+    console.error("[hub] fetchRemoteConfig failure:", err);
+    // Provide a safe fallback to keep the system running.
+    return { featureFlags: {} };
+  }
+}
+
+// --- ORIGINAL LOGIC (refactored) ----------------------------------------
+async function initialize() {
+  const remote = await fetchRemoteConfig();
+  // Simplified data‑driven flow – no deep nesting.
+  const flags = { ...remote.featureFlags };
+  // Example of flat conditional using the validated data.
+  if (flags.enableBeta) {
+    // Small‑viable value: enable beta only when explicitly set.
+    startBetaMode();
+  } else {
+    // Explicit else satisfies Defensive Execution.
+    startStableMode();
+  }
+}
+
+// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+initialize().catch((e) => {
+  // Final safety net – any uncaught error is logged and does not crash the process.
+  console.error("[hub] Fatal initialization error:", e);
+  process.exit(1);
+});
```
```

// src/utils/validateEnv.ts
import process from 'node:process';

/**
 * Verify that all required environment variables are present at startup.
 * Throws if any are missing – fail fast to avoid hidden bugs.
 */
export function assertEnvVars(required: string[]) {
  const missing = required.filter((key) => !Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(process.env, key));
  if (missing.length) {
    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variables: ${missing.join(', ')}`);
  }
}

// src/lib/schema.ts
import { z } from 'zod';

/**
 * Typed schema for the YAML configuration used by the Hub.
 * Enforces shape at parse time, preventing deep‑nesting logic errors.
 */
export const hubConfigSchema = z.object({
  hubToken: z.string(),
  maxConcurrency: z.number().int().positive().default(5),
  // add other required fields here
});

export function loadHubConfig(path: string): z.infer<typeof hubConfigSchema> {
  const raw = require('fs').readFileSync(path, 'utf8');
  const parsed = JSON.parse(raw); // In real code replace with a safe yaml parser
  const result = hubConfigSchema.safeParse(parsed);
  if (!result.success) {
    throw new Error(`Invalid hub config: ${result.error.message}`);
  }
  return result.data;
}

// src/workflows/deploy.ts
import { assertEnvVars } from '../utils/validateEnv';
import { loadHubConfig } from '../lib/schema';

/**
 * Orchestrates a deployment step. All external calls are wrapped in try/catch.
 */
export async function deploy() {
  try {
    // 1️⃣ Validate env vars before any work
    assertEnvVars(['HUB_TOKEN', 'PROJECT_ID']);

    // 2️⃣ Load and validate config
    const cfg = loadHubConfig('config/hub.yaml');

    // 3️⃣ Example of a simple loop (brute‑force) over items
    for (const item of cfg.items) {
      try {
        // ... deployment logic ...
      } catch (innerErr) {
        // Log and continue – never let one failure abort the whole run
        console.error(`Failed on item ${item.id}:`, innerErr.message);
      }
    }
  } catch (err) {
    // Centralised error handling – satisfies Defensive Execution
    console.error('Deployment aborted:', err.message);
    // Optional: re‑throw or return a structured error for the caller
    // throw err;
  }
}

### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
export function calculateDiscount(tier: string, amount: number): number {
  const validTiers = ['basic', 'standard', 'premium'];
  if (!validTiers.includes(tier)) {
    throw new Error("Unsupported tier: " + tier);
  }
  const discountRate = tier === 'basic' ? 0.05 : tier === 'standard' ? 0.10 : 0.15;
  const rawDiscount = amount * discountRate;
  // Clamp to never exceed the amount and avoid >100% discount
  const discount = Math.min(rawDiscount, amount);
  // Prevent floating‑point silent errors
  return parseFloat(discount.toFixed(2));
}
```

```typescript
export function validateToken(token: string | undefined): boolean {
  // Defensive: explicit fallback for missing token
  if (!token) {
    return false;
  }
  try {
    const payload = JSON.parse(token);
    if (!payload?.exp) {
      return false;
    }
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    // Guard against negative or past expiration
    if (payload.exp <= now) {
      return false;
    }
    return true;
  } catch {
    // Treat parsing errors as invalid token
    return false;
  }
}

export function updateUserScore(userId: string, delta: number): Promise<void> {
  return prisma.user.update({
    where: { id: userId },
    data: { score: { increment: delta } }
  }).catch((err) => {
    // Defensive catch to avoid silent failures
    console.error('Failed to update user score:', err);
    throw err;
  });
}

// src/services/userService.ts
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as E from 'fp-ts/Either';

export const calculateDiscount = (price: number, quantity: number, discountRate: number): E.Either<string, number> => {
  if (typeof price !== 'number' || isNaN(price) || price < 0) {
    return E.left('price must be a non-negative number');
  }
  if (typeof quantity !== 'number' || isNaN(quantity) || quantity < 0) {
    return E.left('quantity must be a non-negative number');
  }
  if (typeof discountRate !== 'number' || isNaN(discountRate) || discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) {
    return E.left('discountRate must be a number between 0 and 1');
  }
  const subtotal = price * quantity;
  const discountAmount = subtotal * discountRate;
  const total = subtotal - discountAmount;
  if (total < 0) {
    return E.left('calculation resulted in a negative total');
  }
  return E.right(total);
};
```

+ import type { RequestInit } from 'node:http';
+ import fetch from 'node-fetch';
+ import { getEnv } from './env';

+// Defensive fetch wrapper with explicit error handling and env verification
+export async function safeFetch(url: string, init?: RequestInit) {
+  const apiKey = getEnv('API_KEY'); // fail fast if missing
+  const response = await fetch(url, {
+    ...init,
+    headers: {
+      ...(init?.headers || {}),
+      Authorization: `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
+    },
+  });
+  if (!response.ok) {
+    const body = await response.text();
+    throw new Error(`Fetch failed: ${response.status} - ${body}`);
+  }
+  return response.json();
+}
+

+  if (!Number.isInteger(input.age) || input.age < 0) errors.push('Age must be a non‑negative integer');
+  if (errors.length) {
+    throw new Error(`Validation errors: ${errors.join(', ')}`);
+  }
+  return input;

+  if (result.rowCount === 0) {
+    throw new Error('User not found');

export function calculateDiscount(price: number, percent: number): number {
  // Defensive: ensure inputs are valid numbers
  if (typeof price !== 'number' || typeof percent !== 'number' || isNaN(price) || isNaN(percent)) {
    return 0; // fallback value
  }
  const discount = price * (percent / 100);
  // Ensure discount does not exceed price
  const finalDiscount = Math.min(discount, price);
  return finalDiscount;
}

// Property‑based test using fast‑check
import * as fc from 'fast-check';

fc.assert(
  fc.property(
    fc.double({ min: 0, max: 1000 }).chain(p => fc.double({ min: 0, max: 100 }).chain(perc => {
      const result = calculateDiscount(p, perc);
      return result >= 0 && result <= p;
    }))
  )
);

export const TokenPayload = t.type({
  sub: t.string,
  exp: t.number,
  role: t.enum({ admin: 1, user: 2, guest: 3 }),
});

export const isValidToken = (payload: unknown): boolean => {
  const result = TokenPayload.decode(payload);
  if (result._tag !== 'Right') return false; // explicit failure handling
  const { exp, role } = result.right;
  // Defensive: ensure exp is a finite number and not expired
  if (!Number.isFinite(exp) || exp <= Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000)) return false;
  // Substitution‑stable role check – only admin (value 1) is authorized
  return role === 1;
};

```
export const average = (values: number[]): number => {
  // Defensive guard: empty input must not produce NaN
  if (!Array.isArray(values) || values.length === 0) {
    throw new Error('Values array cannot be empty');
  }
  // Simple brute‑force sum; no complex reduction logic needed
  let sum = 0;
  for (const v of values) {
    sum += v;
  }
  return sum / values.length;
};

// Property‑based test (using fast‑check) that previously failed silently:
export const prop_AverageIsBetweenMinAndMax = (arr: number[]) => {
  if (arr.length === 0) return true; // test framework skips empty arrays
  const min = Math.min(...arr);
  const max = Math.max(...arr);
  const avg = average(arr);
  return avg >= min && avg <= max;
};

// The failing case was an empty array that slipped through the guard,
// causing average() to return NaN and the property check to evaluate to false.
// The patch now throws an error, making the failure explicit and preventing
// silent propagation of NaN downstream.
```

import { parseISO, isAfter } from 'date-fns';
export const validateToken = (token: string, now: Date = new Date()) => {
  const payload = decodeJwt(token);
  if (!payload?.exp) {
    return { valid: false, errors: ['Missing exp'] };
  }
  const expiresAt = parseISO(payload.exp);
  const isExpired = isAfter(now, expiresAt);
  if (isExpired) {
    return { valid: false, errors: ['Token expired'] };
  }
  const role = payload.role ?? 'user';
  const permissions = permissionMatrix[role] ?? [];
  return { valid: true, permissions };
};
```

```
async function fetchSpokeData(url: string, token: string): Promise<any> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(url, {
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
    });
    if (!response.ok) {
      // Explicit handling instead of throwing
      return { error: `HTTP ${response.status}` };
    }
    const data = await response.json();
    return data;
  } catch (err) {
    // Catch ensures error is not unhandled
    console.error('Fetch failed:', err);
    return { error: err.message };
  }
}

// Example: simplify data transformation without external library
function normalizePayload(payload: any): any {
  // Brute‑force loop for small n; no complex library needed
  const normalized: Record<string, any> = {};
  for (const key in payload) {
    if (payload.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
      normalized[key] = payload[key];
    }
  }
  return normalized;
}

// Guard against missing env vars at startup
if (!process.env.SPOKE_TOKEN || !process.env.API_BASE_URL) {
  throw new Error('Missing required environment variables: SPOKE_TOKEN or API_BASE_URL');
}

```
export function calculateTax(income: number): number {\n  if (typeof income !== 'number' || !Number.isFinite(income)) {\n    throw new Error('Income must be a finite number');\n  }\n  if (income < 0) {\n    throw new Error('Income cannot be negative');\n  }\n  const brackets = [{limit: 10000, rate: 0.1}, {limit: 40000, rate: 0.2}, {limit: Infinity, rate: 0.3}];\n  let tax = 0;\n  let remaining = income;\n  for (const {limit, rate} of brackets) {\n    if (remaining <= 0) break;\n    const prevLimit = brackets[ brackets.indexOf({limit, rate}) > 0 ? brackets[ brackets.indexOf({limit, rate}) - 1].limit : 0];\n    const taxable = Math.min(remaining, limit - prevLimit);\n    tax += taxable * rate;\n    remaining -= taxable;\n  }\n  return tax;\n}
```

undefined

### Patch
```
// src/api/client.ts
import { strict as assert } from 'assert';
import * as fs from 'fs';
import * as path from 'path';

// ---- 1. Defensive Execution (Hamilton) -----------------------------------
// All public functions now have an `else` branch or a `catch` to guarantee
// that errors are treated as expected data points rather than uncaught exceptions.

/**
 * Loads required environment variables and throws a clear error if any are missing.
 */
function validateEnv(): void {
  const required = ['API_KEY', 'DB_URL', 'LOG_LEVEL'];
  for (const key of required) {
    if (!process.env[key]) {
      // Explicit fallback path – never let a missing var silently become undefined.
      throw new Error(`Missing required env var: ${key}`);
    }
  }
}

/**
 * Wrapper around the Vercel curl command. Uses a simple loop (Brute Force) and
 * defensive error handling to avoid deep nesting or complex conditionals.
 */
export async function callVercel<T>(endpoint: string, payload: unknown): Promise<T> {
  try {
    const response = await fetch(`https://api.vercel.com${endpoint}`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        // Explicitly set only the headers we control; everything else comes from env.
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        ...(process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN}` } : {}),
      },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });

    if (!response.ok) {
      // Expected data point – log and re‑throw a structured error.
      const errBody = await response.text();
      throw new Error(`Vercel API error ${response.status}: ${errBody}`);
    }

    // Simple parsing – no complex conditional logic.
    const data = (await response.json()) as T;
    return data;
  } catch (err) {
    // Defensive catch – ensures the function never propagates an uncaught exception.
    // Instead we wrap it in a known error shape that callers can handle.
    throw new Error(`callVercel failed: ${(err as Error).message}`);
  }
}

// ---- 2. Data over Logic (Pike Rule 5) -------------------------------------
// The schema for the incoming payload is now defined in BACKEND_STRUCTURE.md.
// Any deviation triggers a validation error before logic runs.

export function validatePayload(payload: unknown): asserts payload {
  const expectedKeys = ['userId', 'action', 'metadata'] as const;
  for (const key of expectedKeys) {
    if (!(key in payload)) {
      throw new Error(`Payload missing required field: ${key}`);
    }
  }
  // Ensure `metadata` is an object, not a deep‑nested structure that would
  // require complex conditionals.
  if (typeof payload.metadata !== 'object' || payload.metadata === null) {
    throw new Error('metadata must be a non‑null object');
  }
}

// ---- 3. Simple over Fancy (Pike Rules 1‑4) --------------------------------
// The implementation uses a straightforward loop‑free fetch; no external
// libraries are introduced because `n` (the number of endpoints) is small.

export async function processUserRequest(userId: string, action: string, metadata: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<string> {
  validateEnv();
  validatePayload({ userId, action, metadata });

  // Minimal, brute‑force handling – no deep nesting.
  const endpoint = `/api/${action}`;
  const payload = { userId, metadata };
  const result = await callVercel<{ status: string; message: string }>(endpoint, payload);
  return result.message;
}

// Export for unit‑testing – makes the contract explicit and substitutable (Liskov).
export const PUBLIC_API = {
  processUserRequest,
  validateEnv,
  validatePayload,
};

```

// 1️⃣ Defensive Execution – add explicit error handling
async function fetchConfig(url: string): Promise<Config> {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url);
    if (!res.ok) {
      throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
    }
    return await res.json();
  } catch (err) {
    // Fail fast with a clear message; never let the promise resolve undefined
    console.error('fetchConfig failure:', err);
    throw new Error(`Unable to load config from ${url}: ${err.message}`);

import { fetch } from 'node-fetch';

/**
 * Process a user request with strict type safety and defensive checks.
 */
export async function processUser(input: { data?: { id: string } }): Promise<any> {
  // Validate required environment variable
  if (!process.env.API_BASE_URL) {
    throw new Error('API_BASE_URL is not defined');
  }

  // Ensure a valid user ID is present
  if (!input?.data?.id) {
    throw new Error('User ID is required');
  }

  // Construct URL safely with encoding
  const url = new URL(`/users/${encodeURIComponent(input.data.id)}`, process.env.API_BASE_URL);

  // Perform request with explicit error handling
  const response = await fetch(url.toString()).catch(err => {
    console.error('Network error while fetching user data:', err);
    throw new Error('Failed to reach user service');
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const errorBody = await response.text();
    throw new Error(`User service returned ${response.status}: ${errorBody}`);
  }

  return response.json();
}

// Example usage in a Vercel workflow (run: block)
// const user = await processUser({ data: { id: input.id } });

export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountRate: number): number {
  if (price < 0) throw new Error('Price cannot be negative');
  if (discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) throw new Error('Discount rate must be between 0 and 1');
  const discounted = price * (1 - discountRate);
  return discounted;
}

```typescript
// src/utils/pricing.ts
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as E from 'fp-ts/Either';

/** Safely calculate final price after discount.
 * @param price - base price, must be >= 0
 * @param discount - discount rate (0‑1)
 * @returns Either<ErrorMessage, number> with final price
 */
export const calculateDiscount = (price: number, discount: number): E.Either<string, number> => {
  // Defensive validation
  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || price < 0) {
    return E.left('price must be a non‑negative finite number');
  }
  if (!Number.isFinite(discount) || discount < 0 || discount > 1) {
    return E.left('discount must be between 0 and 1');
  }

  const discounted = price * (1 - discount);
  // Ensure we never return a negative final price
  const finalPrice = discounted < 0 ? 0 : discounted;
  return E.right(finalPrice);
};
```
```

```typescript
function validateAndTransform(input: any): Result {
  try {
    if (!input) {
      return { success: false, error: 'Input is null or undefined' };
    }
    const cleaned = Array.isArray(input.items) ? input.items : [];
    const processed = cleaned.map(item => {
      if (typeof item === 'number') {
        // Guard against overflow by clamping
        return Math.min(Math.max(item, 0), Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER);
      }
      return item;
    });
    return { success: true, data: processed };
  } catch (e) {
    // Defensive catch: never let exception escape
    return { success: false, error: e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e) };
  }
}

## Issue #346: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
```typescript
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountPercent: number): number {
  // Defensive validation – ensure inputs are numbers and within expected ranges
  if (typeof price !== 'number' || typeof discountPercent !== 'number' ||
      Number.isNaN(price) || Number.isNaN(discountPercent)) {
    return 0;
  }

  // Guard against negative or out‑of‑range values
  const safePrice = Math.max(0, price);
  const safeDiscount = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, discountPercent));

  // Compute discount amount, never exceeding the price
  const discountAmount = Math.min(safePrice, (safePrice * safeDiscount) / 100);
  const finalPrice = safePrice - discountAmount;

  // Ensure we never return a negative price
  return Math.max(0, finalPrice);
}
```
```

```typescript
// src/utils/env.ts
import { config } from 'dotenv';
config();

const REQUIRED_ENVS = ['API_KEY', 'DB_URL', 'JWT_SECRET'] as const;

REQUIRED_ENVS.forEach((key) => {
  if (!process.env[key]) {
    throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
  }
});

export const env = {
  apiKey: process.env.API_KEY as string,
  dbUrl: process.env.DB_URL as string,
  jwtSecret: process.env.JWT_SECRET as string,
} as const;

// src/services/userService.ts
import { env } from '../utils/env';
import { db } from '../db/client';
import { UserInput } from '../types'; // explicit type contract

export async function createUser(input: UserInput): Promise<string> {
  // Defensive: validate input shape early
  if (!input?.email || !input?.name) {
    throw new Error('User input missing required fields');
  }

  // Simple brute‑force insert – no ORM magic
  const result = await db.query(
    'INSERT INTO users (email, name, token) VALUES ($1, $2, $3) RETURNING token',
    [input.email, input.name, env.jwtSecret]
  );

  // Every function has an else / catch
  if (!result?.rows?.[0]?.token) {
    throw new Error('Failed to generate user token');
  }

  return result.rows[0].token;
}

// src/workflows/deploy.ts
import { vercel } from '../utils/vercelClient';
import { env } from '../utils/env';

export async function deploySpoke(spokeName: string): Promise<void> {
  try {
    const resp = await vercel.curl(`/${spokeName}/deploy`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${env.apiKey}` },
    });
    // Simple success check – no complex parsing
    if (resp.status !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`Deploy failed with status ${resp.status}`);
    }
  } catch (err) {
    // Catch all errors and surface a clear message
    console.error('Deploy workflow error:', err.message);
    throw err; // re‑throw to let caller handle or log
  }
}
```

```typescript
// src/utils/discount.ts
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as TE from 'fp-ts/TaskEither';

/**
 * Calculates final price after applying a coupon.
 * Throws on invalid inputs to make errors explicit.
 */
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, coupon: number): number {
  // Defensive checks – fail fast
  if (!Number.isFinite(price) || price < 0) {
    throw new Error('price must be a non‑negative finite number');
  }
  if (!Number.isFinite(coupon) || coupon < 0) {
    throw new Error('coupon must be a non‑negative finite number');
  }
  // Business rule: coupon cannot exceed 100%
  if (coupon > 100) {
    throw new Error('coupon cannot be greater than 100%');
  }

  const discountFactor = 1 - coupon / 100;
  return price * discountFactor;
}
```
```

import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';

export const applyDiscount = (price: number, discountRate: number): number => {
  // Clamp discountRate to the valid range to prevent silent negative results
  const safeRate = Math.min(Math.max(discountRate, 0), 1);
  const discountAmount = price * safeRate;
  const finalPrice = price - discountAmount;
  // Defensive else ensures a non‑negative value is always returned
  return finalPrice >= 0 ? finalPrice : 0;
};

// Property‑based test (fast‑check) – placed in tests/discount.test.ts
import * as fc from 'fast-check';

  fc.property(
    fc.double({ min: -100, max: 100 }).chain(price =>
      fc.double({ min: -2, max: 2 }).chain(discountRate =>
        fc.constantFrom(applyDiscount(price, discountRate)).map(final => {
          return {
            final,
            isNumber: typeof final === 'number' && !Number.isNaN(final),
            nonNegative: final >= 0,
            notOverDiscounted: final <= price + 1e-9
          };
        })
      )
    )

    if (!result.properties.every(p => p)) {

## Issue #326: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/326](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/326)

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, couponCode: string): number {
  // Defensive implementation with validation
  if (price <= 0) {
    throw new Error('price must be positive');
  }
  if (!couponCode || couponCode.length === 0) {
    return price; // no discount
  }
  const discountRate = Math.min(couponCode.length % 3, 0.5); // cap at 50%
  const discount = price * discountRate / 10;
  return price - discount;
}
```

## Issue #324: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

**State:** open
**URL:** [https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/324](https://github.com/adamberneche-afk/TSO/issues/324)
**Created:** April 5, 2026 at 03:17 PM

**Description:**
### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
```typescript
// src/utils/discount.ts
import { calculateDiscount } from '../utils/discount';

/**
 * Safely calculates discount percentage.
 * - Rejects negative percentages.
 * - Caps at 100%.
 * - Accepts only finite numbers.
 */
export const calculateDiscount = (input: number | string): number => {
  const num = typeof input === 'string' ? Number(input) : input;
  if (!Number.isFinite(num)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid discount value: must be a finite number');
  }
  const discounted = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, num));
  return discounted;
};

// src/middleware/validateUserId.ts
export const validateUserId = (id: string | number): string => {
  if (typeof id !== 'string' || id.trim() === '') {
    throw new Error('User ID must be a non‑empty string');
  }
  const numericId = Number(id);
  if (!Number.isInteger(numericId) || numericId <= 0) {
    throw new Error('User ID must be a positive integer');
  }
  return numericId.toString();
};

// test/property/discount.test.ts
import * as fc from 'fast-check';
import { calculateDiscount } from '../src/utils/discount';

fc.assert(
  fc.property(
    fc.double({ min: -1000, max: 1000 }), // includes negative and large values
    (value) => {
      const result = calculateDiscount(value);
      // Ensure result is within [0,100]
      return result >= 0 && result <= 100;
    },
    { numRegens: 500 }
  ),
  (failures) => {
    console.error('Discount property test failed', failures);

undefined

### Patch
```
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, tiers: {threshold: number, rate: number}[]): number {\n  // Guard against invalid input\n  if (price == null || isNaN(price)) {\n    throw new Error('price must be a valid number');\n  }\n  // Ensure price is non‑negative\n  const safePrice = Math.max(0, price);\n  // Find applicable tier using >= to include boundary\n  const tier = tiers.find(t => safePrice >= t.threshold);\n  if (!tier) return 0;\n  // Apply rate, avoid floating point accumulation errors\n  const discount = safePrice * tier.rate;\n  // Round to 2 decimal places to avoid floating point noise\n  return Math.round(discount * 100) / 100;\n}
```

### Value Impact
undefined

### Patch
```
export function calculateDiscount(price: number, discountRate: number): number {
  // Guard against invalid inputs
  if (Number.isNaN(price) || Number.isNaN(discountRate)) {
    throw new Error('Invalid input: price and discountRate must be numbers');
  }
  if (price < 0) {
    throw new Error('price cannot be negative');
  }
  if (discountRate < 0 || discountRate > 1) {
    throw new Error('discountRate must be between 0 and 1');
  }
  const discount = price * discountRate;
  const finalPrice = price - discount;
  return finalPrice < 0 ? 0 : finalPrice;
}

```

export function calculateExpiration(issuedAt: number, ttlMs: number): number {\n  const now = Date.now();\n  if (issuedAt > now) {\n    throw new Error('issuedAt cannot be in the future');\n  }\n  const expiration = issuedAt + ttlMs;\n  if (expiration < now) {\n    // Reset to a valid future timestamp\n    return now + ttlMs;\n  }\n  return expiration;\n}

import fetch from 'node-fetch';

interface User {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  email: string;
}

async function fetchUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  if (!id) {
    throw new Error('User ID is required');
  }
  const apiBase = process.env.USER_API_BASE;
  if (!apiBase) {
    throw new Error('USER_API_BASE environment variable is missing');
  }
  const url = `${apiBase}/users/${encodeURIComponent(id)}`;
  try {
    const res = await fetch(url);
    if (!res.ok) {
      const errBody = await res.text();
      throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}: ${errBody}`);
    }
    const data = await res.json();
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') {
      throw new Error('Invalid user data format');
    }
    return data as User;
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Failed to fetch user:', err);
    throw err;
  }
}

function processOrder(order) {
  // Example patch: ensure an else branch
  if (order && order.items?.length) {
    // process items
  } else {
    throw new Error('Invalid order payload');
  }
}

import { env } from '$env/dynamic/public';
import type { User } from '../types';

// Ensure required env vars are present at startup
if (!env.API_URL) {
  throw new Error('API_URL environment variable is required');
}

export async function fetchUser(id: string): Promise<User> {
  const response = await fetch(`${env.API_URL}/users/${id}`);
  if (!response.ok) {
    const errBody = await response.text();
    console.error('API error:', response.status, errBody);
    throw new Error(`API request failed with status ${response.status}`);
  }
  const data = await response.json();
  if (!data || !data.id) {
    throw new Error('Invalid user data received');
  }
  return data;
}
```

import * as fc from 'fast-check';

// Test for rounding errors in calculateDiscount function
fc.assert(
  fc.property(
    fc.double({ min: 0, max: 1000 }).chain(price =>
      fc.constantSized(2, fc.nat(0)).chain(precision =>
        fc.double({ min: 0, max: 1 }).chain(discountRate =>
          const expected = Math.round(price * (1 - discountRate / 100) * 100) / 100;
          const actual = Math.round(price * (1 - discountRate / 100) * 100) / 100; // original may lack EPSILON
          actual === expected
        )
      )
    )
  ),
  { numRuns: 500 }
);

  fc.property(
    fc.array(fc.record({ id: fc.stringAscii() })).filter(arr => arr.length > 0),
    arr => {
      const ids = arr.map(item => item.id);
      const targetId = ids[ids.length - 1];

import { config } from 'dotenv';
config();

const REQUIRED_ENVS = ['API_KEY', 'DB_URL', 'LOG_LEVEL'] as const;

function validateEnv(): void {
  for (const key of REQUIRED_ENVS) {
    if (!process.env[key]) {
      throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${key}`);
    }
  }
}

validateEnv();

export const getConfig = (): { apiKey: string; dbUrl: string; logLevel: string } => ({
  apiKey: process.env.API_KEY as string,
  dbUrl: process.env.DB_URL as string,
  logLevel: process.env.LOG_LEVEL as string,
});

// src/services/dataProcessor.ts
import { getConfig } from '../utils/env';

interface DataItem {
  id: string;
  payload: Record<string, unknown>;
}

export async function processItems(items: DataItem[]): Promise<DataItem[]> {
  const validated: DataItem[] = [];
  for (const item of items) {
    try {
      if (!item.payload || typeof item.payload !== 'object') {
        continue;
      }
      const transformed = {
        ...item,
        payload: {
          ...item.payload,
          processedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        },
      };
      validated.push(transformed);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(`Failed to process item ${item.id}:`, err);
    }
  }
  return validated;
}
```

 export function normalizeInput(values: number[]): number {
   if (values.length === 0) {
     // Silent error: previously returned NaN, causing downstream failures
     throw new Error('Array must contain at least one element');
   }
   const sum = values.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
   const avg = sum / values.length;
   // Guard against division by zero (should never happen but defensive)
   return Number.isFinite(avg) ? avg : 0;
 }

import * as t from 'io-ts';
import * as E from 'fp-ts/Either';

export const transformData = (raw: any): t.struct({ items: t.array(t.type({ price: t.number, tax?: t.number })) }) => {
  const decoder = t.strict({ items: t.array(t.type({ price: t.number, tax?: t.number })) });
  const result = decoder.decode(raw);
  if (E.isLeft(result)) {
    console.error('Invalid payload:', result.left.message);
    return [] as any; // fallback to empty array
  }
  return result.right.items.map(item => ({
    ...item,
    total: item.price + (item.tax ?? 0)
  }));
};
```

// file: src/middleware/validateUser.ts
import { pipe } from 'fp-ts/function';
import * as fc from 'fast-check';

// Updated validation function with explicit edge case handling
export const validateUser = (input: unknown): boolean => {
  // 1. Guard against empty or whitespace-only strings
  if (typeof input !== 'string' || !input.trim()) {
    return false;
  }

  // 2. Enforce max length before regex to avoid ReDoS
  if (input.length > 128) {
    return false;
  }

  // 3. Whitelist allowed characters (alphanumeric, underscore, hyphen)
  const allowedPattern = /^[A-Za-z0-9_-]+$/;
  if (!allowedPattern.test(input)) {
    return false;
  }

  // 4. Range check: age must be between 13 and 120 inclusive
  const age = Number(input);
  if (Number.isNaN(age) || age < 13 || age > 120) {
    return false;
  }

  // 5. Ensure no leading/trailing whitespace after trim
  return input.trim().length > 0;
};

// Property‑based test example (for documentation)
fc.assert(
  fc.property(
    fc.string(),
    (str) => {
      const result = validateUser(str);
      // Silent error: previously returned true for empty strings
      if (str.trim() === '') {
        return !result; // must be false
      }
      // Additional checks could be added here
      return true;
    }
  )
);
```

function groupBy<T, K>(items: T[], getKey: (item: T) => K): Record<K, T[]> {
  return items.reduce((acc, item) => {
    const key = getKey(item);
    (acc[key] = acc[key] || []).push(item);
    return acc;
  }, {} as Record<K, T[]>);
}

      headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${process.env.API_KEY}` },
    });
    if (!response.ok) {
      // Expected data point – treat non‑2xx as a valid outcome
      return { error: `HTTP ${response.status}`, data: null };
    }
    const json = await response.json();
    return { error: null, data: json };
  } catch (err) {
    // Proactively surface the failure as structured data
    return { error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err), data: null };
  }
}

## Issue #295: CTO HUB: HUNT Action

### Patch
```
import { clamp } from 'lodash';
export function applyDiscount(price: number, discountPercent: number, rounding: 'up'|'down'|'nearest' = 'nearest'): number {
  if (price < 0) {
    throw new Error('Price cannot be negative');
  }
  if (discountPercent < 0 || discountPercent > 100) {
    throw new Error('Discount percent must be between 0 and 100');
  }
  const multiplier = 1 - discountPercent / 100;
  const discounted = price * multiplier;
  const rounded = rounding === 'up' ? Math.ceil(discounted * 100) / 100 : rounding === 'down' ? Math.floor(discounted * 100) / 100 : Math.round(discounted * 100) / 100;
  return clamp(0, Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER, rounded);
}
```

export function validateTokenExpiration(ts: number, maxAgeMs: number): boolean {
  const now = Date.now();
  const expiry = ts + maxAgeMs;
  // Guard against clock skew causing false‑negative expiration
  if (now - Date.now() > 5_000) {
    return false;
  }
  return now < expiry;
}

 export function hasPermission(user: User, action: string): boolean {
  const perms = user.roles.reduce((acc, role) => {
    acc[role] = true;
    return acc;
  }, {} as Record<string, boolean>);
  // Ensure 'admin' role always grants permission
  if (perms.admin) return true;
  return !!perms[action];
}

 export function calculateCartTotal(cart: CartItem[]): number {
  // Use BigInt to avoid overflow on large sums
  const total = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + BigInt(item.price * item.qty), 0n);
  // Cast back to number only if it fits safely
  if (total > Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER) {
    throw new Error('Cart total exceeds safe integer range');
  }
  return Number(total);
}
